<script>
    window.imaginodata = {
        page: json.parse('{\u0022route\u0022:\u0022home\u0022,\u0022site:lang\u0022:\u0022fr\u0022,\u0022site:domain\u0022:\u0022shs\u0022,\u0022component\u0022:\u0022pages.home-page\u0022}'),

<script data-navigate-once>
    window.addeventlistener('load', function() {
        'use strict';

        const imagino_script_id = 'imagino-script';
        const imagino_consent_name = 'imagino';

        async function createscripttagimagino(onload) {
            return new promise((resolve) => {
                if (document.getelementbyid(imagino_script_id)) return resolve();
                const script = document.createelement("script");
                script.onload = () => resolve();
                script.type = "text/javascript";
                script.async = true;
                script.src = "https://tag.imagino.com/jzgfzrelqdcsb8cfbfiwoa==/api.js";
                script.id = imagino_script_id;
                document.body.appendchild(script);
            });
        }

        function removeimagino() {
            if (window.imaginotag) delete window.imaginotag;
            const script = document.getelementbyid(imagino_script_id);
            if (!script) return;
            script.parentnode.removechild(script);
        }

        function callimagino() {
            if (!window.imaginotag) return;
            const tracker = window.imaginotag.gettracker();
            tracker.identify(null);
            tracker.identify(window.imaginodata.page.iduser);
            tracker.page(
                window.imaginodata.currenturl,
                window.imaginodata.page,
            );
        }

        window.consents.registerandcall(async (hasconsentimagino) => {
            if (!hasconsentimagino) return removeimagino();
            await createscripttagimagino();
            callimagino();
        }, imagino_consent_name);

        document.addeventlistener('livewire:navigated', async () => {
            if (!await window.consents.get(imagino_consent_name)) return;
            callimagino();
        });
    });
</script>

    (function() {
        'use strict';

        const helpscout_script_id = 'helpscout-beacon-script';
        const helpscout_consent_name = 'helpscout';

        
        window.beacon = function(method, options, data) {
            window.beacon.readyqueue.push({
                method: method,
                options: options,
                data: data
            });
        };
        // initialisation d’une file d’attente vide
        window.beacon.readyqueue = [];
        window.domhelpscoutscript = null;

        function inithelpscout() {

            function injectbeaconscript() {
                if (window.domhelpscoutscript) return;

                const script = document.createelement("script");
                script.type = "text/javascript";
                script.async = true;
                script.src = "https://beacon-v2.helpscout.net";
                script.id = helpscout_script_id;
                window.domhelpscoutscript = script;

                document.body.appendchild(script);
            }

            // si le document est déjà complètement chargé, injection immédiate du script
            if (document.readystate === "complete") {
                return injectbeaconscript();
            }
            // sinon, attendre la fin du chargement de la page
            if (window.attachevent) {
                // compatibilité internet explorer <= 8
                window.attachevent("onload", injectbeaconscript);
            } else {
                // navigateurs modernes
                window.addeventlistener("load", injectbeaconscript, false);
            }
        }


        
        const helpscoutkey = '47bdae06-bbc4-484c-9e7c-01489e1a8fc2';

        document.addeventlistener('livewire:navigating', () => {
            beacon('destroy');
        });
        document.addeventlistener('livewire:navigated', () => {
            window.consents.registerandcall((hasconsenthelpscout) => {
                if (!hasconsenthelpscout) {
                    beacon('destroy');
                    return;
                }
                inithelpscout();
                window.beacon('init', helpscoutkey);
            }, helpscout_consent_name);
        });
    })();
</script>
        
            </body>
</html>
